NOTICE

MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

FORM No. 155

Members’ Voluntary Winding Up
TECHNO STEEL PROCESSING INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED
Notice convening final meeting of contributories
Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a general meeting of the members of the above named Company
will be held at No. 2, (Old No. 23), 1st Floor, Ramakrishna Nagar, 2nd Main Road, R.A. Puram,
Chennai-600 028, Tamil Nadu on the 20th day of October 2014 at 11.30 A.M. for the purpose of having an account laid
before them showing the manner in which the winding up has been conducted and the property of the company
disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special
resolution of the company, the manner in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator
shall be disposed of.
For JAIN, CHRISTOPHER, SRIKANTH & SRIKANTH,
Chartered Accountants.
Chennai,
11th September, 2014.

SRIKANTH BALAKRISHNAN,
Liquidator of Techno Steel Processing India
Private Limited.

CANCELLATION OF ADOPTION
I, adopted S. Sharmila D/o. Thiru S. Udayakumar & Tmt. V. Kavitha born on 12th May 2007 (native district:
Cuddalore), residing at No. 25-C, 408 Quarters, Neyveli, after executing an adoption deed on 27th May 2007 as I did not
have a child then and named her as S. Sanjana Shivani, which was published in Tamil Nadu Government Gazette
Part VI-4 Issue No. 42, dated 31-10-2007 at page No. 1350. But, now, as I have two children of my own. We decided
to cancel the adoption deed mutually and through II Additional Subordinate Judge, Cuddalore Court Order
(O.S. No. 65/2013), we got the above adoption cancelled. By this S. Sanjana Shivani can now assume her old name and
shall be called as U. SHARMILA.
Neyveli,
12th September, 2014.

K. SARAVANAKUMAR,
Foster Parent.

CIN: U45201TN2005PTC058220
Notice by Company of Members’ Voluntary Winding up and
Appointment of Liquidator.

At the Extraordinary General Meeting of the company duly convened and held at its Registered Office on Wednesday
the 3rd September, 2014 the Equity Shareholders have passed Special Resolution for:(i)

Voluntary winding up of the company under Section 484 (1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and for appointment
of Mr. R. SRIDHARAN, Director, as the Liquidator in terms of Section 490 of the Companies Act, 1956 and
for fixing his remuneration.

(ii)

Authorizing the Liquidator to do all such acts, deeds and things as may be necessary for winding up the affairs
of the Company and distributing its assets.

Chennai,
12th September, 2014.

For SRI RANGA HOLDINGS PRIVATE LIMITED,
